## 3. API Reference

### 3.0 RSNC v4.0 Status

#### GET /api/rsnc/v4/status
Returns the current state of the four-tier RSNC v4.0 engine, including the Phyto-Resonome layer status, Phoenix progress, and Оё_K attention weights.

**Response:**
```json
{
  "version": "4.0",
  "phoenix_progress": 0.85,
  "phoenix_stage": "warming",
  "phoenix_tau": 52.9,
  "tier_stats": {
    "tier_0": { "size": 2048, "frozen": true, "name": "Universal" },
    "tier_1": { "archetypes": 8, "centroids_per": 256, "name": "Archetype" },
    "tier_2": { "delta_bound_min": 0.05, "delta_bound_max": 0.25, "name": "Personal" },
    "tier_3": { "compounds": 8, "active_protocol": "Ecklonia_Cava", "name": "Phyto-Resonome" }
  },
  "fusion_weights": {
    "milestone": 3,
    "universal": 0.3,
    "archetype": 0.45,
    "personal": 0.25
  },
  "theta_k_attention": {
    "enabled": true,
    "angle": 128.23,
    "layer_freq": 119.74
  },
  "archetype_assignments": {
    "dominant": "ALPHA_NAVIGATOR",
    "weights": [0.6, 0.1, 0.05, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.2, 0.05]
  }
}
```

### 3.1 Phyto-Resonome APIs

#### GET /api/rsnc/phyto-compounds
Returns phytochemical compounds with their effect vectors.

**Response:**
```json
[{
  "compoundId": 1,
  "name": "Ecklonia Cava Phlorotannin",
  "species": "E. cava",
  "primaryGeneSymbols": ["BDNF", "NRXN1", "HTT", "KIBRA"],
  "gosFrequency": 176.59,
  "archetypeAffinity": [6, 3], // KAPPA_MEMORY, DELTA_EMPATH
  "mechanism": "5-HT2A partial agonist / anti-inflammatory",
  "dosageMg": 25.0,
  "halfLifeHours": 3.0,
  "contraindications": ["SSRIs", "lithium"]
}]
```

#### GET /api/rsnc/phyto-recommendation
Returns personalized compound recommendation based on current archetype weights.

**Response:**
```json
{
  "recommendation": { "compound": "Ecklonia Cava Phlorotannin", "rationale": "High affinity for KAPPA_MEMORY and DELTA_EMPATH, targeting BDNF and KIBRA for memory consolidation." },
  "protocol": {
    "name": "Theta-Linguist Enhancement",
    "phase1": "500mg + Bacopa 300mg",
    "phase2": "Ashwagandha 600mg",
    "phase3": "Maintenance Microdose"
  },
  "expectedImprovement": 0.15
}
```

### 3.2 Core Data APIs

#### GET /api/thoughts
Returns all thought stream entries.

**Response:** `Thought[]`

#### GET /api/resonome
Returns AUBREY 62-gene resonome data.

**Response:** `ResonomeGene[]`
```json
[{
  "id": "uuid",
  "symbol": "SHANK3",
  "chromosome": 7,
  "category": "language",
  "frequency": 212.38,
  "phaseAngle": 45.2,
  "rune": "бҡҰ",
  "hieroglyph": "р“ҠҪ"
}]
```

### 3.3 Engine APIs

#### GET /api/engine/frames
Returns recent engine frames with RSNC v4.0 metadata included.

**Response:** `EngineFrame[]`

#### POST /api/engine/frames
Ingest a new engine frame from the GOS pipeline.

**Request Body:** Raw pipeline output.

**Response:** `201 Created`

## 4. Database Schema

### 4.0 Phyto-Resonome Tables

#### phyto_resonome
| Column | Type | Constraints | Description |
|--------|------|-------------|-------------|
| compound_id | SERIAL | PK | Auto-increment ID |
| name | TEXT | NOT NULL | Compound name |
| species | TEXT | NOT NULL | Plant species |
| traditional_use | TEXT | NOT NULL | Traditional usage |
| primary_gene_symbols | TEXT[] | NOT NULL | Target gene symbols |
| gos_frequency | REAL | NOT NULL | GOS resonance frequency |
| gos_phase | REAL | NOT NULL | Phase angle |
| archetype_affinity | INTEGER[] | NOT NULL | Indices of archetypes |
| mechanism | TEXT | NOT NULL | Mechanism of action |
| dosage_mg | REAL | NOT NULL | Recommended dosage |
| half_life_hours | REAL | NOT NULL | Biological half-life |
| contraindications | TEXT | nullable | Known contraindications |

#### compound_gene_effects
| Column | Type | Constraints | Description |
|--------|------|-------------|-------------|
| id | SERIAL | PK | Auto-increment ID |
| compound_id | INTEGER | NOT NULL, FK | Parent compound |
| gene_symbol | TEXT | NOT NULL | Target gene |
| effect_type | TEXT | NOT NULL | e.g., upregulate, inhibit |
| strength | REAL | NOT NULL | 0.0-1.0 scale |
| mechanism_notes | TEXT | nullable | Detailed mechanism |

#### archetype_protocols
| Column | Type | Constraints | Description |
|--------|------|-------------|-------------|
| protocol_id | SERIAL | PK | Auto-increment ID |
| archetype_index | INTEGER | NOT NULL | Target archetype (0-7) |
| name | TEXT | NOT NULL | Protocol name |
| phase_1 | TEXT | NOT NULL | JSON string |
| phase_2 | TEXT | NOT NULL | JSON string |
| phase_3 | TEXT | NOT NULL | JSON string |
| waveforms | TEXT | NOT NULL | JSON string |
| expected_improvement | REAL | NOT NULL | Expected gain % |
| min_days | INTEGER | NOT NULL | Duration |
| created_at | TIMESTAMP | NOT NULL | Creation time |

### 4.1 Core Tables (RSNC v4.0 Updates)

#### personal_codebooks
| Column | Type | Constraints | Description |
|--------|------|-------------|-------------|
| user_id | UUID | PK | Unique identifier |
| archetype_weights | REAL[] | NOT NULL | Weighted mixture of archetypes |
| delta_matrix | BYTEA | NOT NULL | Serialized О”(u) tensor |
| delta_norm | REAL | NOT NULL | Current norm |
| **lambda_current** | **REAL** | **NOT NULL** | **Current adaptive bound** |
| **phoenix_progress** | **REAL** | **DEFAULT 0** | **Convergence metric (0-1)** |
| fusion_weights | REAL[] | NOT NULL | [ОұвӮҖ, ОұвӮҒ, ОұвӮӮ] |
| version | INTEGER | DEFAULT 1 | Codebook version |
| last_updated | TIMESTAMP | NOT NULL | Update time |

#### neural_archetypes
| Column | Type | Constraints | Description |
|--------|------|-------------|-------------|
| id | UUID | PK | Unique identifier |
| archetype_index | INTEGER | NOT NULL | 0-7 index |
| name | TEXT | NOT NULL | Archetype name |
| primary_biomarker | TEXT | NOT NULL | Primary EEG biomarker |
| genes | TEXT[] | NOT NULL | Associated gene list |
| population_pct | REAL | NOT NULL | Population percentage |
| gos_frequency | REAL | NOT NULL | GOS layer frequency |

## 6. Integration Guide

### 6.1 Connecting Phyto Integration

To integrate the Phyto-Resonome layer with the training pipeline:

1.  **Map Compounds:** Link `compound_gene_effects` to archetype index.
2.  **Synchronize Frequencies:** Ensure compound intake aligns with GOS target frequencies (e.g., Apigenin вҶ’ HTR2A 176.59 Hz).
3.  **Apply Protocol:** When `archetype_index` changes or `phoenix_progress` lags, retrieve `archetype_protocols` via `/api/rsnc/phyto-protocols`.

### 6.2 Monitoring the RSNC v4.0

Use the **Phoenix Progress** metric (API `/api/rsnc/v4/status`) to monitor system health.
*   **P < 0.3 (Cold):** User is initializing.
*   **0.3 вүӨ P < 0.95 (Warming):** Personal delta is learning.
*   **P вүҘ 0.95 (Calibrated):** Personal codebook is optimal.

**Fallback Trigger:**
If `delta_norm` hits the `lambda_current` bound constantly, trigger a Phyto recommendation via `archetype_protocols`.
